A pool was specially built so that the reflection of the circular hotel on the pool forms a closed loop on the water surface. Standing on the platform on the seventh floor of the front desk, you can perfectly record the night view of the Sheraton Hotel. It is beautiful.

Self-driving guests should park their cars in the parking lot on the first or second floor, and then take the elevator to the seventh floor front desk to check in. It is recommended that the hotel set up a clear sign at the entrance to the mountain, telling everyone to go to the parking lot first, and then take the elevator to the seventh floor, so as not to drive up the mountain in a daze, and then drive back down the mountain to the parking lot on the first floor.

posted:Posted November 15, 2023
msg:South Taihu Villa is a uniquely charming garden-style and manor-style tourist resort hotel in Huzhou City. It is a state guesthouse with a state-owned enterprise background. It is located on the eastern slope of Xiaomei Mountain in the remnants of Bian Mountain in the gentle and elegant Taihu Lake Tourist Resort in Huzhou, close to the southern shoreline of Taihu Lake. The terrain is higher in the west and lower in the east, with a drop of more than 40 meters. The villa covers an area of ‚Äã‚Äãmore than 60,000 square meters and integrates accommodation, catering, recreation, conference and other service facilities. It is only a 10-minute drive from the center of Huzhou and 4 kilometers away from Taihu Longemont Paradise and Taihu Tuying Ecological Wetland Cultural Park. Walking into the unique and charming Nantaihu Villa, you feel as if you have entered a beautiful paradise, with lush trees and the fragrance of flowers. Here, you can feel the simplicity from nature, experience the true return to simplicity, completely forget the irritability of the city, and enjoy the beauty of the lakes and mountains. Here, you can watch the sunrise in the morning and hear the chirping of birds and the waves; watch the scenery of lakes and mountains in the afternoon, enjoy sailing boats and blue waves; watch the vastness of the stars and rivers at night, and enjoy the moonlight and breeze. Here, you can see the gorgeous night light show of Moon Bay Plaza from the viewing platform in the lobby of the villa. In particular, you can see the colorful patterns and reflections in the water transformed by the "ring"-shaped building of the Sheraton Hot Spring Resort Hotel decorated with exterior wall lights. Like a crescent moon painted with color. Here, the balcony of the lake view room faces the "Ring"-shaped building opposite. It really opens the door to the lake, and you can admire the moon through the window. Here, when you climb to the Taihu Tower on the top of Xiaomei Mountain, you can overlook the beautiful scenery of South Taihu Lake and the newly built Taihu Dragon Dream Paradise, and you can take pictures of the beautiful sunset (if the weather is good).
The staff at South Taihu Villa have a strong sense of service and are kind, enthusiastic and thoughtful. In particular, Li Bingbing, the GRO manager of South Taihu Villa, contacted us in advance and took the initiative to help us solve various problems we encountered during check-in. He repeatedly taught us how to use the facilities in the room, often asked us what we needed, and promptly provided the hot water in the room. The problem was reported to the engineering depar**ent and solved promptly; she took the trouble to lead us to visit other room types of South Taihu Villa and Guanhu Wentang Resort Hotel, and gave good publicity and promotion to the Villa and its hotels. The full-time housekeeper Zou Qifang not only disinfected the room we were about to stay in beforehand, gave us fruits, and distributed a large amount of drinking water, but also immediately organized the waiters to move and adjust the mattress after knowing that our waists were not suitable for soft mattresses. , so that we can have a better bed rest, so that we can spend the entire holiday happily and comfortably.
The young men in the concierge depar**ent who drive battery cars and are responsible for picking up and dropping off in the park are responsive to all requests and answer all questions. Their performance is very eye-catching! The morning buffet not only has many varieties, but also has many Huzhou specialty pastries and snacks, which are of good quality. The dishes in the Chinese restaurant are famous for their three treasures of Taihu Lake: white fish, white shrimp and whitebait. They not only allow guests to taste fresh food from the lake, but also savor the long-standing cultural charm of Taihu Lake.
In the golden autumn season, Huzhou is the most beautiful, and South Taihu Villa is the most beautiful!
